World's Eyes Focused on Berlin: Anglo-German Negotiations Begin; Representatives from Both Sides Gather at the Chancellery, with Hitler Personally Participating in the Deliberations 50

(Berlin) Berlin is the focal point of the world today, as the long-awaited meeting between British and German statesmen, whose outcome is expected to have a far-reaching impact on European peace, is now underway. British Foreign Secretary Simon, Lord Privy Seal Eden, and British Ambassador to Berlin, Phipps, drove to the Chancellery at 10:30 this morning. After exchanging customary greetings, they immediately began discussing substantive matters. The German representatives are Chancellor Hitler, Foreign Minister Neurath, and disarmament envoy Ribbentrop. According to well-informed sources, Ribbentrop's participation indicates that disarmament and compulsory military service will be major topics of discussion. The talks were suspended during lunchtime and will resume in the afternoon. (Reuters, 25th)

The talks will continue tomorrow. Simon will fly back to London on Wednesday or Thursday, while Eden will travel to Moscow, then Warsaw and Prague. He is expected to return to London on April 4th.

The results of this trip will be reported to the Cabinet and Parliament by the two officials. On April 11th, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, French Foreign Minister Laval, and British Foreign Secretary Simon will meet in Stresa to discuss the overall situation based on the reports of the British Foreign Secretary and Eden. (Reuters, 25th)

(Berlin) Regarding the international negotiations on European issues, which began last Saturday in Paris, British Foreign Secretary Simon and Lord Privy Seal Eden will first hold their first talks with German Foreign Minister Neurath here at 10:00 today. Then, German Chancellor Hitler will meet with the two British statesmen. Last night, the British Embassy held a reception for the two British cabinet members, and today, Foreign Minister Neurath will host a formal welcome. Tomorrow, the British Embassy will invite German Chancellor Hitler, all German cabinet members, and British guests to a public banquet, followed by a reception hosted by Hitler. (National Telegraph, 25th)

(Berlin) According to Simon, the British cabinet members met with Foreign Minister Neurath for only half an hour this afternoon, and the discussion was purely procedural. It is generally believed that Eden has already informed Neurath of the results of the Paris trilateral talks this afternoon. Neurath replied that the German people believe in the British cabinet members and believe they will understand Germany's needs. (Havas, 24th)

Discussion of Issues Can Be Divided into Two Parts

The British community here believes that the main purpose of the discussion is to exchange views rather than seek practical compromises. It is said that German diplomats intend to divide the issues discussed into two parts: one is issues that can be resolved with an exchange of conditions, such as the air pact and naval matters; the other is issues that are extremely difficult to compromise on, such as compulsory military service, the Eastern Locarno Pact, and the Austrian question. The colonial question and Germany's cession of Memel to Lithuania under the Treaty of Versailles are unlikely to be discussed, as the former would make the talks more complicated. Simon's purpose in seeking consultation is limited to European security and does not want to cover these matters. The British community considers Memel to be a matter for the League of Nations to handle.

The Eastern European Pact is the Most Difficult

Regarding the air pact, no difficulties are expected because Germany also urgently wants to establish it. The same is true for naval matters. Germany's ambition in this regard today is not as great as it used to be. According to unofficial opinions, Germany would be satisfied with a navy of 400,000 tons, including some submarines. The most difficult issue is the Eastern Locarno Pact. According to a Reuters interview with a senior official, mutual assistance clauses seem impossible to accept at present. It is also said that Germany does not seem willing to give up its interests in Austria, and Hitler himself pays particular attention to this. As for compulsory military service, the number of new troops has not yet been determined, and negotiations are possible. (Reuters, 25th)

German View: Hostility Towards the Soviet Union

(Berlin) Well-informed sources in the British community here believe that Hitler is currently making a large-scale effort to lure Britain into Germany's political trap. It is generally remembered that Lord Lothian, secretary to former Prime Minister Lloyd George, and Lord Allen of Hurtwood, a confidant of Prime Minister MacDonald, visited Berlin in January this year and met with key figures in the German government, bringing back reports detailing Germany's political conspiracies. These reports have not yet been published. The content states that Germany's main idea is to hate the Soviet Union, considering it a deep moral enemy. To compromise with Soviet Russia would be a "crime of destroying culture." These are Hitler's own words. Therefore, Hitler may even propose concluding a trilateral pact between Britain, the United States, and Germany to mutually guarantee against external aggression. To show that this pact is not directed against France, he also intends to explicitly recognize Germany's western border and the existing borders between Germany and Poland, Czechoslovakia, Belgium, and the Netherlands. In this way, Britain can avoid the Eastern European mutual assistance pact, and the Soviet Union will be effectively isolated. Regarding the Danube Pact, Germany intends to accept recognition of Austria's independence without reservations, asserting that "if the Austrian people wish to merge with Germany, they should have the opportunity to clearly express their will." The implication is that the activities of the German National Socialist Party should not be considered interference in Austria's internal affairs, just as the activities of the Austrian Heimwehr should not be considered interference in Italy's internal affairs.

Equal Demands for the Army, Navy, and Air Force

In addition to the above, Germany also demands three things: (1) Germany's military equipment should be equal to that of the most powerful land army in Europe; (2) Germany's air force strength should be equivalent to that of Britain, provided that the British air force is equal to the most powerful air force in Europe; (3) Germany should have a navy of 400,000 tons. Regarding the last point, according to Lord Lothian's observation, Hitler seems not unwilling to compromise, only demanding that the German navy dominate the Baltic Sea while allowing Britain to control all the oceans. This plan was learned from the British side. It is not yet possible to determine whether Hitler's proposed plan has changed substantially in these Anglo-German talks. However, it should be stated that the British Foreign Office spokesman believes that this plan is unacceptable. (Havas, 25th)

Optimism on the British Side Regarding the Future of the Talks

British officials in Berlin have a cautiously optimistic attitude towards the outcome of the Anglo-German talks, but they have clearly stated that the purpose of the discussions is not to make suggestions or concessions, but to gather information. The German side believes that Hitler's main purpose is to make the British representatives, Simon and Eden, understand Germany's current foreign policy, especially Germany's suspicion of Soviet Russia. Germany now has spiritual and political reasons to regard Soviet Russia as a major enemy that the Western powers cannot harmonize with. There is no doubt that Soviet Russia poses a danger to other Western powers. A strong Germany is the best European barrier to defend against this danger. This is an important part of today's German diplomatic negotiations and will likely be presented to the British representatives today.

Several optimistic observers have proposed that Britain, Germany, and the United States conclude a mutual guarantee treaty and recognize Germany's eastern and western borders to isolate Soviet Russia. However, some have clearly stated that this kind of imagination cannot currently gain support from political circles. German newspapers also seem to be optimistic. Today, the Deutsche Tageszeitung said, "The meeting has begun under auspicious signs." (Reuters, 25th)

A Glimpse of British Officials' Visit to Germany: Hitler Sends Black Guards to Welcome Distinguished Guests, with Continuous Cheers from the Public Along the Way 51

(Berlin) Eden and Simon met in Amsterdam and then flew to Germany together, arriving at Tempelhof Airport at 5:34 last night. The British flag was hung in the middle of the two German flags at the airport. Several of Hitler's trusted Black Guards were stationed at the airport to welcome them, showing respect. German Foreign Minister Neurath, British Ambassador Phipps, and other dignitaries all stepped forward to pay their respects when the plane landed. The crowd also cheered enthusiastically. After Simon exited the plane, the Black Guard commander drew his saber and approached Simon, standing at attention and saying, "Hitler's Guard is here to welcome Your Excellency." Simon smiled and raised his hat in reply. Then, the group boarded the waiting cars and went to the British Embassy. The crowd along the way was like a wall, gathering on Wilhelmstrasse to watch the distinguished guests. The British Embassy was also packed. Thousands of people gathered in front of the Hotel Adlon, where the two distinguished guests were staying. The streets through which the cars passed were filled with cheers, and many people shouted "Long live!" The situation was the same when the two distinguished guests went from the British Embassy to the hotel. When they arrived at the hotel, other guests and the crowd outside cheered. (Reuters, 25th)

(Berlin) British Foreign Secretary Simon and Lord Privy Seal Eden arrived safely at Tempelhof Airport here on a large Imperial Airways aircraft today at 5:30 PM, precisely on schedule. The visit of these British dignitaries is of great importance to the future of the world. The importance of its nature has been conveyed to the entire German public through newspapers, radio, and newsreels in the past week. Therefore, tens of thousands of German people welcomed the British guests at the airport. Simon was the first to open the plane door and descend amidst the cheers of the crowd. He was followed by Eden. German Foreign Minister Neurath and other government officials had been waiting on the field for half an hour and immediately stepped forward to greet them. Neurath and Simon talked to each other at the airport with a very friendly and sincere attitude. Chancellor Hitler sent his personal guard to guard the field. When the British guests got off the plane and passed in front of the guards, the commanding officer stepped forward to salute and report the task of guarding the field. Many government officials were present to greet them today. They had arrived at the visitors' area since the afternoon, and the lawn was already full. Those who arrived later had almost no place to stand. British Ambassador to Germany Phipps also led the entire staff of the embassy to welcome them. Other German dignitaries included Meissner, Secretary of the Chancellor's Office and Hitler's personal representative, Buelow, Secretary of the Foreign Office, and Bassewitz, Director of the Treaty Department. Many German and foreign journalists were also present, especially British reporters. When the British guests left the airport, Foreign Minister Neurath and British Foreign Secretary Simon boarded the first car, and British Ambassador Phipps and Lord Privy Seal Eden boarded the second car, one after another, to the Hotel Adlon, where they would be staying. When they drove away, the cheers at the airport had not yet subsided. (National Telegraph, 24th)

(Berlin) Simon and Eden received an enthusiastic welcome along the way as they drove from the British Embassy to the Chancellery this morning. Many women shouted "Long live!" and the men saluted in the style of the National Socialist Party. When the two left the embassy, several sound film cameramen and newspaper photographers gathered in front of the embassy to work. Then, they entered a beautiful black car and drove in, a distance of only 500 yards. (Reuters, 25th)

(Berlin) British Foreign Secretary Simon and Lord Privy Seal Eden are here to try to stabilize the disturbing situation caused by Germany's rearmament. Their prospects have encountered obstacles. British and French Newspaper Commentary 59

(London) With Foreign Secretary Simon about to meet with German Chancellor Hitler, newspapers are paying particular attention to the following two points: First, Germany needs to recognize the sanctity of treaties, as this is an indispensable condition for organizing a peace mechanism. Second, Foreign Secretary Simon's mission is limited. Although this trip is very important, it has not adopted a firm resolution. The Daily Telegraph states, "Foreign Secretary Simon and Lord Privy Seal Eden do not intend to haggle between Britain and Germany; nor are they plenipotentiary ambassadors of the united front of Britain, France, and Italy. Foreign Secretary Simon claims that his mission is only exploratory in nature, as if exploring the geological structure layer by layer in order to delve into the deepest layer of the international collective system. On the German side, even the most stubborn of the National Socialist leaders may not expect to release another shocking thunderbolt just one week after the previous bombing. We believe that if we consider the procedure set by Britain calmly, the consensus of opinion between Britain, France, and Italy is not difficult to restore, and the communiqué issued after the Paris talks the other day is enough to dispel the last remaining worries. As for the task of advising Germany to return to the League of Nations, it should be based on a strong spirit and realistic circumstances, and cannot be achieved by empty words. Germany should make sincere efforts to ease the situation, which cannot be forced. However, acts that undermine the Treaty of Versailles, such as what happened ten days ago, must not be repeated in the future." (Havas, 25th)

(Paris) Newspapers are still uneasy about the Berlin talks between British and German cabinet members, fearing that Germany will make formal concessions to Britain while trying to alienate Britain and France on matters that are difficult for France to accept. Le Petit Parisien writes, "We can easily guess that Germany will propose several suggestions that the United Kingdom would like to hear in order to lure the United Kingdom, such as enthusiastically participating in the Western European air pact, especially that the armaments of various countries should have a certain limit." Le Journal writes, "If the arms limitation treaty is based on the condition of equal rights for the signatory countries, Germany will certainly not refuse to participate. Germany may even propose the principle of general arms reduction as a cover for its deception. In other words, after Germany implements compulsory conscription, its military quota has exceeded that of neighboring countries, and neighboring countries should not conclude alliances to defend themselves. However, Germany's concessions must have certain conditions, and Germany cannot recognize other countries' conclusion of similar alliance pacts, France's political and military rapprochement with Soviet Russia." Le Jour says, "It is generally said that Germany intends to make some formal concessions to please Britain, such as rejoining the League of Nations. Has Britain felt too accommodating towards Germany's concrete gestures, and should it not exchange symbolic gestures again in the future?" (Havas, 25th)

French Chamber of Deputies Passes Naval Construction Bill 64

(Paris) The Chamber of Deputies discussed the naval construction bill and passed it by a vote of 453 to 125, authorizing the Ministry of the Navy to begin construction of one battleship before December 31 this year to replace an old ship. At the same time, it will also build two torpedo boats. In addition, it is authorized to spend 785,000,000 francs on battleship construction, 148,000,000 francs on torpedo boat construction, and 132,000,000 francs on the purchase of accessories and materials between 1935 and 1939. (Havas, 25th)

(Paris) The Chamber of Deputies discussed the naval construction bill this morning. Stein, the reporter for the Chamber's Naval Committee, stated the reasons why France's battleships should be replaced, saying that France's three Voltaire-class battleships, with a ship age of 24 years, three Jean Bart-class battleships, with a ship age of 22 years, and three Lorraine-class battleships, with a ship age of 19 years, for a total of 185,785 tons, are all obsolete or equal to scrapped ships. However, the new ships built in 1935, including torpedo boats, are only 34,400 tons, costing about 928 million francs. In addition, if new ships are not built, the number of shipyard workers who lose their jobs will reach 2,000. At this point, Socialist deputies proposed postponing the discussion of the bill. After Navy Minister Pietri clarified, the Chamber rejected the Socialists' proposal by a vote of 413 to 160. Stein continued to say that France had proposed a maximum limit of 25,000 tons per battleship, but the United States, Japan, and Italy were all building 35,000-ton battleships, and the cost of France building a battleship fleet was perhaps four times less than the cost of building an auxiliary fleet. The construction bill will continue to be discussed this afternoon. In addition, the passive air defense bill will also be discussed this afternoon. (Havas, 25th)

US Mysterious Plane Test Flight: Invincible Warship in the Air; Strong Combat Power; Able to Fly 3,000 Miles in One Go 65

(Washington) If the US mysterious plane test flight is successful today, the US Air Force will have even more advantages. The Associated Press has learned that the test flights are currently being conducted by naval experts, simultaneously on the east and west coasts. One large aircraft is currently being tested in Alameda, California, and another is being tested by experts in Norfolk, Virginia. Officials are keeping the contents of this aircraft strictly secret. The Associated Press has learned that the new aircraft has a wingspan of 100 feet and is equipped with attack and military equipment. Its combat power is similar to that of a battleship. The engine has 830 horsepower and is equipped with six machine guns. Its rear can be loaded with two tons of powerful bombs. The entire aircraft requires eight people to operate. Naval experts say the new aircraft can fly 3,000 miles non-stop. If the test flight is successful this time, the Navy will build 30 more of these new aircraft and divide them into three teams, sending them to Pearl Harbor in Honolulu and the west and east coasts. (National Telegraph, 24th)

Explosion at a Munitions Depot in Harbin: Residents Felt Like the End Was Near and Hid in Cellars for Eight Hours 69

(Harbin) A munitions depot in the suburbs of Harbin exploded at 11:00 am yesterday. The explosions did not stop, and black smoke filled the air, as if it were being bombarded. Residents feared that the end of the world had arrived and hid in cellars for eight hours. Houses were shaken and heavily damaged, with some collapsing. The amount of loss is yet to be estimated. "Manchukuo" and Japanese troops risked their lives to rescue and extinguish the flames. The exact number of deaths and injuries is currently unknown, but the number of deaths is not expected to be as high as several dozen. The authorities are currently investigating the cause of the fire. However, a Reuters reporter heard that various explosives had been stored in the depot for many years, and internal heat had caused the disaster. Fortunately, a large batch of highly explosive materials had recently been moved elsewhere. The authorities plan to build a new modern munitions depot to prevent further explosions. People are now prohibited from walking within 30 yards around the munitions depot, fearing that unextinguished embers may cause further explosions. (Reuter's Telegram, 25th)

Joint Air Defense Between the United States and Australia: The Content of the Plan as Reported by Japan 73

(Tokyo) The disarmament conference scheduled to be held this year, due to the results of the London preparatory meeting, saw the positions of Japan, Britain, and the United States diverge greatly. As a result, all countries expect a naval arms race to materialize and have already begun various expansions of military equipment. According to information received by the Ministry of the Navy, the Australian government and the United States jointly established a plan to expand the air force. The main content is as follows: At the British military conference held in Singapore earlier, it was decided that when Australia is attacked by other countries from the northern sea, the 3rd Flying Squadron of New South Wales should arrive at Darwin within a considerable period of time after receiving the first warning. However, the Australian government, feeling the necessity of organizing a strong air force to supplement the weakness of the national air force, jointly established a major air force expansion plan with the United States to be completed before 1936 as part of the British Empire's Pacific defense plan. Thirty-six of the latest bombers and fighters were sent from the UK, of which eighteen have already arrived in Australia, and the rest will be dispatched successively within eighteen months. The Philippines Adopts Bimetallism: Pittman Believes There Is a Possibility and Is Optimistic About the Future of Philippine Independence 76

(Washington) Senator Pittman, chairman of the Senate Foreign Relations Committee, predicted today that the Philippines may implement a bimetallic currency system. Pittman said that Filipinos are accustomed to using silver as currency, but the Philippines produces gold worth about 10 million yuan each year. The Philippines has very developed commerce with countries that use gold and silver, which is also conducive to adopting a bimetallic system. However, Filipinos have no difficulty in using the current gold exchange standard, because their financial position makes the currency systems of all countries in the world inferior. When asked about Japan's lack of attention to the silver issue compared to other countries, Pittman replied that the Japanese manage foreign exchange and support their export trade better than any industrial nation. The Japanese can raise or lower the value of the yen within 24 hours, while no foreign country can manipulate the yen. Regarding the amendment of the Philippine Independence Act, Pittman said that the bill includes mandatory and non-mandatory provisions. If Filipinos request to amend the non-mandatory parts of the Independence Act, their attitude before and after would inevitably be inconsistent. However, so far no one has been heard to make such a request, and the current Congress will not discuss the Philippine issue. Finally, Pittman said that the Philippine autonomous constitution is still feasible, and the future of the Philippines is optimistic. (National News Agency Telegram, 24th)

Londoners are Pessimistic About the Gold Standard: Saying That Belgium Abandoning Gold is Only a Matter of Time 77

Mei Lanfang's Troupe Achieves Great Success in Russia: Every Time Mei Performs, the Audience Cheers 78

(Moscow) Dr. Mei Lanfang's Chinese troupe gave its official premiere in Moscow yesterday. Radek wrote in Izvestia about his impressions of seeing Mei's performance: "I am a layman when it comes to Chinese drama. I do not know whether it is so different from the struggle of painful life and Chinese customs as shown by the first performance of the Mei Lanfang Troupe. What we saw tonight was completely different from what we know. We are not familiar with the Chinese language and the unique habits of Chinese drama. However, Mei's performance is truly amazing. This person, using a language that is unfamiliar to us, playing the role of a female character, can intoxicate the audience with his magical art, while at the same time producing vivid and believable images. Mei's expressive eyes and the slender gestures of his hands and body make people forget everything, all of which are different from us. Mei's genius can convey centuries of thought, making it understandable to the general public. As for these dramas themselves, they are not only different from our lives, but also unrelated to the Chinese working masses. However, they make us all the more compelled to convey our thoughts to the great Chinese people and their struggle. The genius shown by the Chinese troupe, its love and dedication to labor, if it can be used for the liberation of the Chinese nation, then China will be able to free itself from its shackles and create its new and great art. This kind of art will definitely not be a pure imitation of Western art, but will be able to use the skills and great experience of ancient Chinese art." In conclusion, Radek expressed his sincere welcome to Mei and his companions for being able to show the genius of the Chinese nation in the Soviet Union, and for the Soviet Union's deep sympathy for China's ongoing liberation struggle. Pravda reported that the Chinese troupe's first performance was deeply noted and praised by the Moscow public. The public warmly welcomed the great actor Mei Lanfang, proving that this performance was not an ordinary performance, but a gathering of the world's oldest culture, namely Chinese culture, and the world's youngest and most progressive culture, namely socialist culture. "This glorious performance of the Chinese troupe has become a joyful festival of our cultural alliance, and at the same time, it has become a commemoration of this great actor. Dalian Correspondence: After the signing of the illegal transfer of the Chinese Eastern Railway, the Japanese and puppet regimes are actively handling the various procedures for the takeover. At this time, Omura Takuichi, Director of the Kwantung Army Transportation Supervision Department and concurrently Director of the Kwantung Bureau Supervisory Department, along with two Councilor officers, Muraji and Inoue, visited various agencies in Lushun and Dalian as the Director of the Supervisory Department for the first inspection. After arriving in Dalian by train at 1:30 PM on the 15th, Omura Takuichi and others greeted those who welcomed them, and then took a car to the Communications Bureau to inspect the telephone, postal, and telegraph offices, and held discussions with the cadres. Then they stayed at the Yamato Hotel. Regarding the important issues such as the Chinese Eastern Railway after the takeover and the Japanese-puppet postal treaty, Omura Takuichi made the following statement: "After the takeover of the North Railway (i.e., the Chinese Eastern Railway), the railway line will become a major artery for Japan in Manchuria. It can exert great authority in terms of military transportation convenience, and if there is a change in the situation. It should strive to absorb transportation of cargo and passengers during peacetime. In the future, it will be operated uniformly under a consistent policy with other lines, so that it can be subject to the effect of overall control, and it can be determined to use this as a major line in the world's industrial transportation field to fully exert its function. For track modification, to make the north and south consistent, we are currently working on the southern branch line, repairing the line on the one hand, and hoping to obtain economic development in the future in sequence. As for the east and west lines, due to the operation of international trains, it is also necessary to regulate the matters of joint transportation between 'Manchukuo' and the Soviet Union after the takeover. Technical negotiations will be conducted soon, and agreements can also be reached. Furthermore, after the takeover, starting from the dispatching of vehicles, the reconstruction of the station in 'Xinjing' and Harbin, and other facilities along the line will be gradually carried out. What is most concerned about the takeover of the North Railway is the development of the industry of 'Manchukuo,' which is linked to this trunk line, so the promotion of the development of industries in the remote areas of northern Manchuria, the supplementation of social facilities, the cultivation of the line's automobile roads, water transport and the extension of air routes can all be fully planned and considered. It is like other 'national' lines, which should also be consistently consistent throughout, and cooperate with the policy of control. As for the matter of the Japan-'Manchukuo' postal treaty, the specific plan is currently under review in the 'central government,' and the local side also hopes for its early realization, and is in the state of promoting it. Although the correct date for this cannot be stated, it is hoped that it will be established in the near future, because it is based on special relations, although it belongs to the problem between Japan and 'Manchukuo,' it is actually related to international affairs, so the foreign affairs authorities are deeply pondering with a legal point of view, and are always proceeding with a cautious attitude."

Omura Takuichi, Director of the Kwantung Army Transportation Supervision Department and concurrently Director of the Kwantung Bureau Supervisory Department, also visited Zhoushuizi Airport, Dalian Metallurgical Company, Wakakusayama Observatory, Maritime Affairs Bureau, and South Manchuria Railway on the 16th with Muraji and Inoue. The bridge piers and foundations of the bridge have long been weak. If a new building is built, the construction cost will be about 12 million yuan, which is difficult to raise such a huge amount of money at one time. As for the modification of the line, the southern branch line has been scheduled to start implementation on August 1 of this year. As for its method, 30 employees are assigned per kilometer, totaling 1,200 people. Yuehan Railway / Zhushao Project is Approaching Completion / Sixty-Five Kilometers of Track Have Been Laid / Expected to Open to Traffic by the End of the 25th Year 113

Guangzhou Correspondence: The Guangzhou-Shaozhou southern section of the Yuehan Railway has been completed and opened to traffic. The project of the section from Shaozhou to Zhuzhou is also progressing actively. A joint meeting of the three sections of the Yuehan Railway was held here recently to discuss the standardization of all equipment and regulations of the entire line to facilitate intermodal transport in each section. Regarding the Zhushao section project, according to Ling Hongxun, Director of the Zhushao Railway Bureau, it has been more than a year since the Zhushao Railway Bureau moved from Guangzhou to Hengzhou. In this year, all 406 kilometers from Zhuzhou to Lechang have started construction. There are more than 100,000 workers working along the road. Recently, about 75% of the earthwork and stonework of the entire section has been completed, about 70% of the tunnels have been completed, about 90% of the retaining walls have been completed, and about 40% of the large and small bridges and culverts have been completed. Zhuzhou, Hengzhou, and Lechang have laid a total of about 65 kilometers of track, and the rest is still being laid. The Guangdong section of the Zhushao section project is the most difficult, because the upstream of the Beijiang River is full of rocky mountains, the route is winding, there are many tunnels, and the water level is shallow, which is not conducive to transportation. The mountain valleys are full of miasma. It is estimated that more than 50 kilometers from Lechang to Pingshi have been under construction since the 22nd year. The ground work has been largely completed, and more than 30 kilometers of track have been laid northward from Lechang. However, there has been a lot of rain in recent months, and the mountainsides have collapsed, which has inevitably affected the project. It is expected that it will take another three months to complete. At that time, the engineering vehicle will directly reach Pingshi, and the project can be considered a small success. Above Pingshi, there is a highway through southern Hunan, leading to Hengzhou and Changsha. For the time being, the highway and railway are intermodal transport, and north-south traffic will be more convenient. As for the Zhushao section railway project, if there are no obstacles, it is expected to open to traffic by the end of the 25th year. In addition, the joint meeting of the three sections of the Yuehan Road continued to be held on the 18th and 19th. If the discussion of each case is completed, it can be closed on the afternoon of the 19th. (March 19)

Jiangsu Province Postpones the Handling of House Tax / The Ministry of Finance Has Already Consulted the Jiangsu Provincial Government 114

The Jiangsu Provincial Government announced the regulations on collecting house tax in various counties, which aroused repercussions among the people of the province. After the Yunjian Fellow Villagers Association in Beijing jointly telegraphed the National Government Yuan and the Ministry of the Yangshu Suzhou, Wujin, Wuxi, Yixing, Jiangyin, Taixian and other fellow villagers associations, the chambers of commerce and public groups of various counties in the province unanimously fought for the cancellation. Early telegrams were sent one after another. Now it is heard that the Executive Yuan has handed over the telegrams from all parties to the Ministry of Finance for verification, and the Ministry of Finance has consulted the Jiangsu Provincial Government, saying "House tax is a legal tax revenue of the local government, but it concerns the burden of the people. At this time, the collapse of rural areas, the withering of commerce, and Jiangsu Province suffered a disaster, it should be carefully considered. Now that the government order has just been issued, and the petitions have come one after another, it is not in line with public opinion, and the regulations for collecting house tax have not been approved by the Ministry for transfer and deliberation, which is not in line with the provisions of Articles 3 and 4 of the National Government's Ming Order on June 25 last year on the reorganization of tax and donation methods and the Ministry's Provisional Law on Supervising Local Finances. It should temporarily postpone the implementation of the newly revised house tax regulations to alleviate the hardships of the people." It is said that the provincial government will respect the Ministry's consultation and withdraw its order for this house tax collection regulation.

In addition to the funds allocated by the National Economic Commission, the shortage will be subsidized by the Jiangxi Provincial Government. In the future, when the hospital is completed, the health equipment in Jiangxi Province will be more perfect.

Songjiang / Fire Brigade Members Tender Collective Resignation 117

The members of the entire city and township of the first, second, third, and fourth districts of this county's Fire Brigade, because members Li Rui and Yao Chongfu were sued to the judiciary by Yin Shisheng, the owner of the Public Confluence Amusement Park opened last year, for sabotage, and transferred to the Shanghai Local Court for trial, and the public prosecution was established after several court sessions, and the plaintiff incidentally requested compensation for losses of more than 10,000 yuan. A meeting will be held on the 26th to discuss disposal measures, widely issue declarations, and send letters to fire brigades in other cities. However, after the No. 1 District Office approved the association's letter to collectively resign, District Chief Li believed that the city river was being dredged in this area and the local fire protection was very important. He specially reported to the county government for verification, and citizens from all walks of life were also very worried.

Suzhou / Guanghua Theater Vandalized 119

The Guanghua Theater outside Panmen was opened by Duan Jinsheng and others. At about 8:00 on the evening of the 24th, when the performance was in progress, more than 30 people wearing gray uniforms suddenly came in to watch the play. After sitting for a while, they swarmed onto the stage, dragged and beat the male and female actors and tea servants, and completely smashed the scenery and equipment before leaving. Suddenly, twenty or thirty people holding rifles reappeared in the theater, smashed the objects for the second time, beat the staff, and fired several shots into the sky as a demonstration. The director of the theater, Duan, immediately reported to the police district in charge. Zhu patrol leader led the police to mediate to no avail. At that time, more than 30 male and female actors fled into the police district in charge. Unexpectedly, several people broke into the police district with great momentum, and dragged the dispatched Zhu Liansheng to the road and beat him. He was seriously injured and sent to Guangmin Hospital for treatment. The doors and windows of the guardhouse on the main road were also damaged. The Third Branch immediately sent a flying squad to suppress it, and the perpetrators had all dispersed. The stores on the road were once closed, and the situation was very tense for a while. It didn't stop until about 9:00. At that time, the injured included the stage director Chen Gengquan, female role Wang Liyun, Muqin Fang, and accountant Shi Yaohui, etc. After investigation, it was found that the perpetrators were guards from the military prison and are still under investigation.

Wuxi / Clash Breaks Out During Gambling Arrest at Anyang Mountain 120

Anyang Mountain, north of Luquqiao Town in the fourth district of the county, has a majestic shape. In the past, Mo Tianyou, a deputy general of Zhang Shicheng, fought fiercely with the Ming army here. The surrounding earthen fort is towering and the river is surrounded. There are many strange caves and rocks on the mountain, and there are four temples. The day before yesterday was the date of the farmers' festival. Farmers from the four villages went to the mountain to worship, claiming to be 100,000, and handicrafts from nearby villages also gathered here. According to old custom, two plays were performed. Unexpectedly, someone named Liu forced the town chief to report to the county government, and the county magistrate ordered Li Zilong, the patrol officer of the public security branch in charge, to handle it according to the situation. Li immediately led the police to the front of Cuiwei Temple and saw a gambling stall spreading out. He immediately intervened and overturned the gambling stall. More than 200 yuan of bets placed by gamblers on the table were snatched away in the chaos. The villagers immediately rioted. With a cry, thousands of people surrounded the police. As more and more people gathered, the police were unable to break through, so they fired three shots into the sky. When the tourists heard the gunfire, they were even more frightened, crying and shouting loudly, and the order was disrupted. A corner of the wall of Cuiwei Temple was collapsed, injuring one old and one young each. The police took advantage of the situation and went down the mountain and fled to the town office to take refuge. The villagers picked up flat burdens and hoe handles on the stall and chased after them. Two policemen were hit in the head by flying stones. Then the town chief tried his best to persuade the crowd. As a result, the injured treated themselves, and Li patrol officer compensated half of the damaged tables and benches before peace was restored.

After the speech, he sent the Public Security Bureau to custody and ordered the resolution of major robbery cases in the county. Unexpectedly, Gao Gui suddenly died violently in custody at about 5:00 pm today (24th). Director Zhang immediately reported to the county by telephone. It was also learned that today (24th), his wife, Fan, sent food to the bureau, and Gao talked with him for a long time. Gao cried bitterly, and after his wife left, Gao expressed to Zhang Qing'an, who was in custody with him, that he had been abiding by the law in recent years. Although he died this time, no one extended his grievances. He couldn't close his eyes and entrusted Zhang to give his family considerable assistance in the future because of his daily colleague's friendship. During this sighing conversation, his complexion changed suddenly and he died. In another investigation, the province has another case of suspicion involving Gao Gui, ordering the county to send Gao Gui to the Security Office for interrogation. Gao heard about it, so he suddenly died violently.

She念[sic] has no interest in life and suddenly has the thought of severing the world. Last night (22nd), she hanged herself to death in the room. Customs Patrol Boat Haihe Sinks, Crew Rescued, Military Supplies Preserved 137

The Haihe, a customs patrol boat assigned by the Jianghai Customs to the Minhai Customs in Fujian last year, encountered fog and drifted while anchored on its way from Shanghai to Fujian this time, resulting in running aground. The general situation has been reported in yesterday's newspaper. Here is a more detailed report:

From Shanghai to Fujian

The Haihe patrol boat, assigned by the Jianghai Customs to the Fujian Minhai Customs, has a displacement of 1,200 tons. The hull was built by the Gaochang Temple Jiangnan Shipyard. When the Customs built five ships last year, this ship was one of them. Its task is to patrol the coast to prevent smuggling and tax evasion. After the ship was completed, it was ordered by the Customs to patrol the Minhai area. The captain is an Englishman named Puhert. There are 38 officers, sailors, and others on board. The ship last came to Shanghai from Fujian for routine repairs at the Jiangnan Shipyard. It was completed and left the factory on the 21st of this month, and sailed back to Minhai from Shanghai.

Truth of the Accident

After the Haihe patrol boat left Shanghai, at 7:30 PM on the 23rd, it had passed the Yanggang Port of Fuzhou and was about to reach Xiamen. The location was at 119 degrees and 42 minutes east longitude and 25 degrees and 42 minutes north latitude. At that time, it was dusk and the sea surface was dark and unclear, resulting in the wrong course. Also, due to fog on the sea, the ship mistakenly ran aground on a reef. The bottom of the ship was broken by the reef, and seawater rushed in. Fortunately, the ship was half-stuck on the reef at the time, so it did not sink immediately, but the situation was very dangerous.

Dispatching Ships for Rescue

After the accident, the shipowner immediately sent a telegram for help. At that time, Taikoo's Yuezhou ship and China Merchants' Haiheng ship received the Haihe's SOS call, and the Xiamen Customs patrol ship Chunxing also received this call for help, and immediately rushed to rescue. Therefore, Yuezhou and Haiheng did not go. When the Chunxing ship arrived at the accident site, the Haihe ship had already been half-submerged in the sea. The Chunxing ship sent sampans to the sea to rescue all 38 crew members of the Haihe ship to its own ship. The three-pound cannon, three machine guns, and the officers and soldiers' pistol bullets on board were also rescued to the Chunxing ship.

Ship Sunk

After the crew and officers of the Haihe ship escaped danger, the water had flooded to the upper deck. Fortunately, there were reefs underneath to support it, so the deck was still exposed. The Chunxing ship was ordered to stay near the Haihe to protect it, to prevent bandits from taking advantage of the lack of ship protection to board the ship and dismantle items. It is heard that the Customs believes that the damage to the ship from running aground is not significant, and it was newly built not long ago, so it has decided to salvage it. The total loss is estimated at 60,000 to 70,000 yuan.

Xiamen, 25th dispatch, reports that the Customs patrol boat Haihe left the province on the 24th and sank near Wuyu Island near Xiamen at night. On the morning of the 25th, Xiamen sent personnel and requisitioned ships to rescue the crew and return. The ship was newly built and the loss is estimated at 500,000.

Ling Hongxun Arrives in Shanghai, Talks About the Imminent Completion of the Guangdong-Hankou Railway, The Entire Line Expected to Be Completed by the End of Next Year, Ling and Others Will Go to Beijing to Discuss the Opening of the Railway with the Ministry of Railways 138

Ling Hongxun, Director of the Zhushao Section of the Guangdong-Hankou Railway Engineering Bureau, and Yin Deyang, Director of the Hunan-Hubei Administration, and a group of nine people, arrived in Shanghai on the Changxing Company's Empress of Japan ship the day before yesterday. They are scheduled to go to Beijing today or tomorrow to discuss the opening of the entire Guangdong-Hankou Railway with the central government and the Ministry of Railways, and to report on the progress of the project. The reporter of the Shen Shi News Agency interviewed Mr. Ling at the inn and received the following details:

Mr. Ling and His Party Arrive in Shanghai

The construction of the Zhushao section of the Guangdong-Hankou Railway began in the 22nd year and has now been largely completed. The entire line can be opened to traffic by the end of next year. On the 18th of this month, the directors of each section of the railway held a meeting in Guangdong to discuss the opening of the entire line. Ling Hongxun, Director of the Zhushao Section of the Engineering Bureau, Yin Deyang, Director of the Hunan-Hubei Section Administration, and Wang Xicheng, Commissioner of the Ministry of Railways, and a group of nine people, because of important official duties, must consult with the central government and the Ministry of Railways and report on the progress of the entire Guangdong-Hankou Railway project. They arrived in Shanghai from Guangdong the day before yesterday and are scheduled to go to Beijing to visit the authorities today or tomorrow to discuss everything.

Current Status of the Zhushao Project

According to Mr. Ling, who told the reporter yesterday, the Zhushao section of the Guangdong-Hankou Railway project started in July of the 22nd year. All the roadbed and other projects for the 406 kilometers between Zhuzhou and Lechang have been fully started. The number of workers participating in the project along the line has now reached 100,000. As of recently, 75% of the earthwork project for the entire section has been completed, 70% of the tunnel project has been completed, 90% of the retaining wall has been completed, and 40% of the culvert and bridge project has been completed. In summary, 60% of the entire project has been completed. The Guangdong side of the project is more difficult, but now the track laying north of Lechang has reached more than 30 kilometers. In two or three months, the construction vehicle will be able to reach Pingshi.

Full Line to Open Next Year

Mr. Ling continued, after the construction vehicle reaches Pingshi, the project for this section can be considered a small success. There is now a highway connecting Pingshi and Changsha. At that time, railway and highway intermodal transport will be carried out first. The entire Guangdong-Hankou route can be reached in three or four days. The three-section meeting held in Guangdong this time has made detailed decisions on the highway connection methods between Guangdong and Hunan provinces. It is expected that the Zhushao section project can be opened to traffic by the end of next year, barring any unexpected obstacles. In these two years, actively prepare all the equipment for the entire line and unify various rules and regulations so that when the railway project is completed, the administration and facilities of the entire line can be unified. In the future, when the entire line is opened to traffic, the three-section railway bureaus will be merged to establish a general management office to unify authority.

Project Cost is 50 Million

Finally, according to Mr. Ling, the Ministry of Railways needs more than 50 million yuan to complete the entire Guangdong-Hankou line, which is borrowed from the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity fund, with 35 million yuan for labor and 1.65 million pounds for materials. Any deficiencies will be supplemented by the Ministry of Railways. After the entire line is opened to traffic, it will connect to the Ping-Han Railway in the north, becoming a major transportation artery between north and south. It will not only facilitate the transportation of mineral and plant products in the three provinces of Hunan, Hubei, and Guangdong, but also greatly benefit the communication of culture between north and south.

Those present included Yan Zhuang from the Supervisory Yuan, Zong Boxuan from the Ministry of Finance, Lu Shuping from the Municipal Government, Zhang Zi from the Local Court, Fan Jietang from the Municipal Public Debt Fund Management Committee, Xu Jiying from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Ye Fuxiao from the Banking Association, Zhang Mengzhou from the Qianye Association, Jin Wenyuan from the Central Bank, Han Diaoqing from the Bank of China, Mao Shijian from the Bank of Communications, and Cai Zengji, Director of the Municipal Finance Bureau, totaling more than thirty people.

Chairman's Report

After the ceremony was conducted, Chairman Cai first reported that today is the date for the ninth lottery for redemption of the principal of municipal public bonds in Shanghai. These bonds were issued in October of the 18th year of the Republic of China, with a total amount of 3 million yuan. In addition to the principal of 1.68 million yuan that has already been redeemed, the remaining principal is 1.32 million yuan. This time, seven bonds will be drawn, with a principal of 210,000 yuan to be redeemed and interest of 52,800 yuan to be paid. The total principal and interest is 262,800 yuan. All winning bonds and the corresponding interest should be paid by the Central, Bank of China, Communications, and Municipal Banks starting on March 31. Please ask the supervisors to check the bond stubs and the lottery stubs for execution.

Seven Bonds Drawn

After the chairman finished reporting, the supervisors checked the bond stubs and the lottery stubs. Then, the representatives of the Central, Bank of China, and Communications Banks were designated from among the guests to draw the lottery. A total of seven bonds were drawn: "04," "13," "29," "41," "54," "75," and "95." After the chairman reviewed them and the supervisors rechecked them without any discrepancies, the winning numbers were announced on a suspended sign.

Western Landlords Association Held Annual General Meeting Yesterday, Reported on Important Issues Such as Land Value Tax and Rent Reduction, and Re-Elected Beilekeluo and Others as Directors 140

The Dagong News Agency reports that the Shanghai Western Landlords Association held its annual general meeting at 4:00 PM yesterday at the Wu Liande Hall at No. 20 Museum Road. More than thirty members attended. Mr. Sibake presided over the meeting, reporting on important matters such as the collection of land value tax and rent reduction. Then, the directors of this session were elected. Details are as follows:

Land Value Tax Issue

After the meeting began, Chairman Sibake reported that before requesting approval of the accounts, he would like to give a brief report on the work of the committee last year. Everyone should still remember that at last year's annual meeting, I mentioned that the Shanghai Municipal Government would collect land value tax on properties outside the Public Concession, and reported to you that the committee had sent a letter to the Consular Body requesting negotiations, and received a reply from the Consular Body stating that it had negotiated with the authorities and would notify you of the results. Since the last annual meeting, the committee has been working tirelessly on this issue, and has not only presented the entire situation to the authorities, but also publicly announced it to various legal organizations to solicit opinions. As of today, we cannot consider this issue to have a satisfactory solution. The attitude of the authorities of some countries is that although their citizens are not legally obligated to pay this land value tax, they still advise them to pay it. At the same time, we are also certain that some citizens of other countries still refuse to pay this tax. What we are concerned about is that this land value tax may contain unequal treatment. This association does not advocate that land outside the concession should be exempt from all land value tax, which must be stated first. However, this association advocates that this land value tax should not have unequal treatment in nature, and a fair and effective appeal committee should be organized, which must be independent in nature and its views must not be biased, so that the relevant owners can appeal the assessed land value for the collection of land tax. In view of the above, regarding the payment of land value tax, please make your own decisions, but in any case, this payment must be accompanied by a protest, stating that it does not affect the rights of the owner.

Reviewing Land Property

At the annual meeting, someone proposed to review the acreage of land property. The area and acreage in the title deeds are often not accurate because the Public Works Department has re-appropriated roads, and there is no clear statement on the title deeds. This matter is very important, especially when estimating its value for setting up mortgages and borrowing money. The committee has contacted the Public Works Department to make the registered owners aware of the accurate acreage in their registered title deeds. The Public Works Department understands this point and agrees to inform the owners of the acreage collected by the bureau for land tax at any time upon written request.

Rent Reduction Issue

Everyone probably hopes that I will express my opinion on the current rent reduction issue. However, regarding this point, I must state that when this association was first established, it was stipulated that "the purpose of this association is not to confront tenants. This association will not sympathize with landlords if the property is unsanitary or dangerous, and this association will not help members increase rents." The purpose of this association is to study matters that affect real estate and are of a public or semi-public nature. The issue of rent is entirely a personal relationship between tenants and landlords. This association cannot formulate any rules for this issue, because the situation is different in different places and cannot be generalized.

Empty House Tax Issue

I do not agree with the collection of empty house police tax. I should ask everyone to note that the police tax is actually a tax that should be borne by the tenant. The owner has already paid land tax to the Public Works Department based on the assessed land value, and this land tax must be paid regardless of whether the property is occupied or not. Therefore, it seems unreasonable to ask the owner to bear the empty house police tax again.

Real Estate Market

Today's real estate market can be said to be temporarily covered by dark clouds. This situation cannot but be attributed to the rising value of silver, but the important reason is actually related to the Sino-Japanese conflict in 1932. Since that incident, the real estate market has never returned to its original state, especially in the eastern and northern districts. Once credit tightens, the signs of decline become more obvious. Previously, owners mortgaged their properties with heavy interest burdens. Now, they are unable to repay the loans or find other ways to raise money, and creditors often exert pressure, resulting in forced sales. Shanghai currently has too many buildings, and the market is not prosperous, so the number of vacant houses is increasing. However, the population of Shanghai is so large and must continue to increase. The current recession is naturally a temporary state, and the vacant houses will soon be occupied. In the view of this association, real estate price declines are common. Today's situation is still a temporary phenomenon. This association does not believe that the population and status of Shanghai will not continue to increase from now on. The construction of houses is not as enthusiastic as before. In the short term, demand can be met with supply. The meeting adjourned.

Re-Elect Directors

After the chairman finished reporting, the directors of this session were re-elected. The names of the elected were as follows: (transliteration) Beilekeluo, Beikai'er, Qiaoluokemeng, Yituolinmeng, Gedeng, Kaipudeng, Kentuo, Kai'en, Laoke, Luonas, Mahan, Tongnada, Miskeng, Pailansideng, Lubinson, Sedasimis, Spaike, Siyaji, Lipaisun, Huierxun.

Asahi Plane Flew Back to Osaka Yesterday Morning, Mayor Wu and Representatives Arrived to See Them Off 141

The Osaka Tokyo Asahi Shimbun's visiting plane to China was originally scheduled to fly back to Osaka at 9:00 AM the day before yesterday, but because Osaka telegraphed that the weather along the Japanese coast was poor, which could hinder the flight, it was postponed to 8:00 AM yesterday to take off from Longhua Airport and return to Japan. The Municipal Government and the Garrison Headquarters still sent many security teams and police officers to stand guard along Jingji Road, reaching the airport to protect them. Those who went to see them off included Wang Changchun, a specialist from the Municipal Government representing Mayor Wu, as well as Yang Hu, Director of the Municipal Security Department, Li Dachao, Director of the First Department of the Municipal Government, Secretary Zhang Tingrong, Chief of Staff Gan of the Garrison Headquarters, Adjutant Gan, as well as representatives of the Japanese Consulate and the Shanghai Asahi Shimbun, representatives of the Japanese community, and dozens of others. The Public Security Bureau also sent a band to the airport to play music. At around 7:00, the two pilots, Xinye and Tsukakoshi, arrived at the airport to inspect the aircraft. It was discovered that a part of the copper tube for transporting oxygen had been burned out, which prevented the engine from starting. The pilot asked the American engineer from the China National Aviation Corporation to provide equipment, which delayed the originally scheduled departure time by one hour. According to Xinye, who spoke to the reporter from the Central News Agency, the plane will cross the East China Sea and fly directly to Osaka over the Goto Islands and north of Nagasaki, with the entire journey taking about six hours. It should arrive at around 3:00 PM, but the sea flight will only take two and a half hours. At 9:10, the two pilots shook hands with the people who came to see them off and said goodbye one by one, and thanked the engineers from the China National Aviation Corporation. Then, they drove the plane into the air, circled the airport once, and then flew towards the northeast.

The Osaka Electric News Agency reported on the 25th that the Asahi Shimbun plane continued its smooth flight and arrived safely at the Osaka Joto Training Ground Airport at 3:21 PM (2:21 PM Shanghai time), taking five hours and twenty-one minutes, which was earlier than expected.

Shi Qingyang Passed Away Yesterday in Shanghai; Funeral Set for 11 AM on the 28th 142

According to the Central News Agency, Mr. Shi Qingyang, former Chairman of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission, participated in the revolution in his early years and made numerous contributions. After assuming the position of Chairman of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission, he devoted particular effort to planning border affairs, which eventually led to overwork and illness. In mid-February, he requested leave to come to Shanghai, staying at the New Asia Hotel. He sought treatment from traditional Chinese medicine practitioner Wu Peiheng, but his condition did not improve. Relatives and friends often advised him to seek treatment in a hospital, but Mr. Shi declined, citing the high cost of hospital care. Coincidentally, Mr. Huang Musong returned from Tibet, and the Central Government approved Mr. Shi's resignation. Following further persuasion from relatives and friends, he entered Baolong Hospital for treatment on March 10th. After an X-ray examination, it was discovered that his lungs were completely damaged, reaching the final stage of pulmonary disease. He was hospitalized for two weeks without improvement and passed away at 5 PM yesterday. His remains were moved to the Chinese Funeral Home at 6 PM, and the funeral is scheduled for 11 AM on the 28th. Mr. Shi was 57 years old and is survived by his wife, two sons, and seven daughters. His second wife is currently pregnant. His eldest son, Zhenru, is in his hometown of Ba County, Sichuan. His second son went to Italy last year to study at the military academy. His eldest daughter is married to Mr. Pan, the current Director of the Revenue Bureau of Fengdu County, Sichuan. The remaining five daughters and one son are all young and still in school. Mr. Shi's two wives came to Shanghai last week to attend to him during his illness. They were extremely grief-stricken at the Chinese Funeral Home yesterday. Mr. Shi's younger brother, Shi Nanyang, who works for the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission, has come to Shanghai from Beijing, along with Mr. Shi's old friends, Yi Yuchang and Xie Bocheng, secretaries of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission, to jointly handle the funeral arrangements. It is said that Mr. Shi's remains will be buried in Nanjing.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Cables Ministry of Finance: Requesting Exemption of Stamp Duty for Acceptance Bills; Said Bills Are for Relief of the City and More Effective Than Checks 145

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce cabled the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing yesterday, stating, "To the esteemed Nanjing Ministry of Finance, we received letters from the Silk and Satin Industry Association and the Electrical Silk Weaving Factory Industry Association on the 23rd of this month, stating that due to the decline of the silk industry and the exhaustion of finance, the associations are vigorously promoting commercial acceptance bills to improve the lending system and relieve the stagnation of currency. Several members have already implemented it. Whether it can achieve the purpose of increasing currency circulation is still in its initial stage, and no results have been seen yet. However, although this acceptance bill has the name of a bill of exchange, it is different from ordinary bills of exchange remitting money from place A to place B. It is only a basis for the agreed payment period in a transaction between two parties. Therefore, even if this acceptance bill is issued during the transaction, the invoice and receipt still need to be opened and affixed with stamps. According to the stamp tax regulations, only bills of exchange and checks are listed, and there is no special term for acceptance bills. If stamp duty is also affixed according to the bill of exchange example, the amount will be very large, not only will the effectiveness of the advocacy not be seen, but the heavy burden of stamp duty will increase sharply, which is contrary to the original purpose of relieving exhaustion and is difficult to bear. Moreover, the stamp tax regulations list checks, which have been ordered by the Ministry to be suspended, and bank and money shop promissory notes are also not affixed with stamps. Therefore, acceptance bills should also be exempt from stamp duty to save the decline of industry and commerce. We hereby jointly send this letter to your association, earnestly requesting that you forward it to the government for a reasonable request, begging for approval, and ordering that all newly advocated commercial acceptance bills be exempt from stamp duty, which is extremely hoped for. We have found that the city is in extreme difficulty due to the impact of the world economic depression and the bankruptcy of rural areas in the country. Industry and commerce are depreciating, and the dangerous situation is unprecedented. The subordinate associations have reported to your Ministry, requesting relief. On the one hand, due to the financial difficulties of the public treasury, we urge merchants to quickly plan self-help methods. The associations have taken the initiative to try commercial acceptance bills, intending to expand the credit system so that the market can have capital to turn around. This commercial acceptance bill is a matter that has been prepared for implementation recently. The original tax source of stamp duty is inherently unaffected. As for its intention to assist the government and relieve the market, it should be more effective than the checks that have been temporarily exempted from stamp duty in the past. The association's request to be exempt from stamp duty is for the purpose of encouraging the commercial acceptance bills that are being advocated and tried. It is reasonable to telegraph your Ministry for review and approval, which is truly convenient for the public. Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce kowtows."

Ministry of Finance: Reply to the Pippi Silk Tobacco Industry Association; Old System Tax Tickets Permitted for Accommodation Within Three Months 148

The Shanghai Pipi Silk Tobacco Industry Association submitted a request to the Tax Affairs Department on the 12th of this month, stating that during the transition period of Yongding's change to special tax, tobacco products that have paid the old tax and are shipped should be allowed to be offset as before within three months, which has been recorded in this newspaper. It is now known that the association has received a reply from the Ministry of Finance approving it. The original reply is recorded below: "Your presentation has been noted. It is verified that before the special tax was changed in the Tingzhou area of Fujian Province, when local tobacco leaves and their processed tobacco silk from the area were transported into the special tax zone, the first-level special tax authorities at the entry point should levy the special tax. Those who have paid the public sale fee tax in the place of origin are also allowed to verify the evidence and offset the special tax, up to two yuan per piece of 67 city catties. After the special tax on local tobacco leaves in the area is implemented, all local tobacco leaves and their processed tobacco silk that have been paid special tax, when transported and sold to the special tax zones of various provinces, should be verified and released in accordance with the special tax regulations. As for the public sale fee tax receipts printed by the counties in Tingzhou, they should be abolished immediately. This has been communicated by the Ministry successively for compliance. Now, according to the association, Yongding and other areas in Tingzhou have not been changed to special tax for a long time. For all tobacco products that have paid the public sale fee tax and obtained the receipt to ship, when they arrive in the special tax zones of various provinces, please allow them to offset the special tax as before within three months to alleviate the merchants' difficulties. After verification, it is still feasible. It is temporarily allowed to be accommodated, but the old tax certificate should be limited to those who have paid the tax and issued it before February 15th of this year, when the Ministry ordered the abolition of the public sale fee tax receipts in the area. In addition to separate orders, you should immediately inform all colleagues to comply. This reply."

Gong Awei, a native of Pudong, is 52 years old and lives at No. 28 Hongqingfang, Puyutang, Nanshi. He is a coppersmith. Recently, due to the impact of the social downturn, he became unemployed and has not found any business since then. His livelihood has been cut off. He has an opium addiction, so he cannot make a living. At about 6 AM yesterday morning, he suddenly had the idea of ending his life. He secretly went to the Dongjiadu Wharf and jumped into the river, attempting suicide. Resident Association Director, Korean Lee Yong-ro Assassinated; Two Murderers Arrested on the Spot; Lee's Wife Slightly Injured and Unharmed 158

Lee Yong-ro, a director of the Korean Residents Association in this city, lived at No. 16 Yuxing Lane, Dixiwei Road. In addition to Lee's wife, there was also an apprentice in the house. The whole family was only these three people. At about 7 AM yesterday morning, Lee had two friends, also Koreans, who came to visit. At that time, Lee had not yet gotten up. Lee's wife opened the door and welcomed them in. One by one, they went upstairs together. According to the visitors, they were inviting Lee to a meeting. As soon as they reached the top of the stairs and said a word, one of them took out a pistol from his sleeve and fired two shots at Lee, hitting Lee's head. Lee's wife heard the sound and went to see, but she was so frightened that she could not make a sound. One of the murderers took a kitchen knife from the table and cut Lee's wife, but the injury was not fatal and not serious. The two murderers fired two more shots as a warning before escaping. At that time, a chauffeur used by the neighboring house at No. 15 heard the gunshots and went out to see. He happened to see the two murderers fleeing in a hurry. He followed them and reported them to the nearby police on duty, who captured the two murderers and took them to the Linping Road police station for temporary detention. On the other hand, a ambulance was called to Lee's house. Because he was Korean, he was immediately sent to the Japanese Fumin Hospital for treatment. However, because the injury was in a vital area and he lost too much blood, the treatment was ineffective, and he died at 10 AM. Lee's wife was injured in the arm, but it was a minor injury. She was bandaged and discharged from the hospital. The two murderers have now been transferred to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for interrogation. It is learned that one is named Lu Hengdun and the other is Li Kuihu. The Japanese Consulate has sent personnel to extradite them. The police station is afraid that the assassination still has a mastermind or other premeditated criminals. The interrogation situation has not been announced for the time being. However, the mutual assassination of Koreans may have a political background, which is also unknown.

According to Lee's wife, the two people had a letter of introduction from a friend in Nanjing and wanted to see someone named Jin, who received them. Then, a certain husband and another young man also arrived. She felt that the visitors were suspicious, so she shouted for help. One of the two immediately pulled out a gun and shot her husband, hitting him in the back of the neck. Although he was rushed to Fumin Hospital for treatment, he died of his injuries shortly after.?

Recently, the market has been depressed, the economy has been exhausted, stores have closed, and factories have stopped work. Everywhere is like this. It must never be compared with ordinary businesses, which are only profit-oriented. However, the company is taking advantage of its authority and recklessly disregards the fact that industry and commerce are in danger, and is about to increase prices again. The members cannot afford it. The implementation of the new chapter must be approved by the French Public Works Bureau. It is said that the Public Works Bureau’s Public Utilities Committee will discuss this matter on Monday. The new chapter was originally scheduled to be implemented on April 1st, but the Public Concession has no regular meeting before April 1st, so the revised regulations may be distributed to the directors of the Public Concession without holding a formal meeting. Ma Hongkui's Death: Family Disputes Property, Ma's Wife Sues Husband's Brother and Husband's Concubine 161

Ma Fuqi (also known as Gu Fuqi, who married into the Ma family and changed his surname to Ma), a local resident of Doutou Lane, 183 Rue Virmont, French Concession, and his wife, Ma Agui, were rickshaw pullers during their lifetime and contracted for cleaning services in the British and French Concessions and the Nanshi area for many years. They had considerable savings and acquired extensive real estate in the French Concession. As land prices increased year by year, their property also increased to no less than several million. Ma Fuqi and Ma Agui had three sons: Hongkui, Hongsheng, and Honggen, all of whom were married and had children. Ma Fuqi and Ma Agui passed away several years ago, one after the other. Their business was inherited by their three sons, and the eldest son, Hongkui, managed the estate without dividing it. Unfortunately, Hongkui died of lung disease on the twelfth day of the eighth month of last year (the third day of the seventh month of the lunar calendar), joining his parents in the afterlife. He left behind his wife, Chen, his concubine, Wang, a son named Lusen, and two daughters named Luying and Luzhen, all of whom are young. They are currently being raised by their uncles, Hongsheng and Honggen. Recently, Hongkui's widow, Ma Chen, suddenly hired lawyers such as Wang Yintai and filed a lawsuit in the Criminal Division of the Second Special District Local Court, accusing her husband's brother, Ma Honggen, and her husband's concubine, Wang Ada (also known as Ma Yuezhen), of encroaching on the estate. She requested that they be interrogated according to the law. The court, based on the complaint, specially opened the Second Criminal Division yesterday morning at 10:30, presided over by Judge Qiu Huanxing, to summon and examine the parties. Both sides arrived with their lawyers. First, the plaintiff, Ma Chen, stated that she was 40 years old, a native of Shanghai, and currently residing in Guifu Lane, Baer Road. The judge asked, "What are you accusing the defendants of?" She replied, "I am accusing them of swallowing my husband's share of the estate." She explained that after her parents-in-law died, the estate was not divided. On the third day of the seventh month of last year, when her husband was dying, his concubine, Wang Ada (also known as Ma Yuezhen), forcibly took her husband's Shanghai Bank safe deposit box key, seal, and bankbook and gave them to her third brother, Honggen. At this point, her lawyer stood up and stated on behalf of Chen that the case was divided into two parts: (1) The plaintiff's husband had a private fortune of about 500,000 in gold, including two boxes of gold pounds, each box seven inches long, two inches high, and three inches wide, and two bankbooks with a total of 26,000 yuan, as well as stacks of ten-yuan banknotes about ten feet long, totaling over 200,000, all stored in bank safe deposit boxes, which were later taken by the defendants. (2) The plaintiff's parents-in-law's estate included real estate in Kangji Lane, Kandi Road, and Gujia Garden, as well as a jointly operated cleaning business in the British, French, and Chinese areas, which generated tens of thousands of gold coins per month, and many rickshaws, totaling a fortune of two to three million gold coins. There were many types, and it was impossible to count them all at once." The judge asked Ma Chen how much the estate was worth. She replied that it was about four million. When questioned, the defendant Ma Honggen stated that when his elder brother Hongkui was ill and died, he was recuperating in Hangzhou. Upon hearing the news, he came to Shanghai. The lawyer Lu Zhenyu handed over all the keys managed by his elder brother to the old accountant Fan Sanduo, together with the plaintiff Chen and her brother Guangyu, to go to the Shanghai Bank and open all three safe deposit boxes belonging to his elder brother for inspection and registration. However, at that time, because the space in the safe deposit box room was small, he stood far away and did not know the details of all the items in the boxes. Later, the plaintiff and lawyer Wang went to open it again. Moreover, all the property in the family after my mother's death was managed by my elder brother and the old accountant Wan Sanduo, and I never interfered. Wang Ada (also known as Ma Yuezhen) stated that she was Hongkui's concubine. When her husband was dying, Chen wanted to seize the key to the silver box, but her husband refused. Later, he handed it over to Wan Sanduo for safekeeping. After her husband died, there was only 30,000 yuan in property, and there was a will stating that it should be divided into three shares, with the woman and Chen each receiving 10,000, and the two daughters, Luying and Luzhen, each receiving 5,000. At this point, the judge summoned the witness Wan Sanduo, but his son came on his behalf, saying that his father was ill and could not come to court. The court then instructed that the witness Wan Sanduo's home would be visited by the court this Wednesday for questioning, and the hearing would be rescheduled. The plaintiff's lawyer requested the court to detain the defendants or order them to post bail. The defendant's lawyer objected, saying that the defendants had a high status and that the plaintiff had not provided any detailed evidence for the charges, so there was no need for detention. The judge also argued that detaining the defendant and ordering bail was a matter for the judge to weigh and should not be disputed. He also announced that the hearing would be adjourned until April 6 and then adjourned.
