Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talking Points

Liu Feifei is Not a Movie Fan 224

— Meng Ruo

The death of the movie star Ruan Lingyu has evoked great sympathy from many people in society. According to recent reports, a young woman from Hunan, Liu Feifei, was extremely indignant upon learning of Ruan Lingyu's suicide. She believed that Zhang Damin and Tang Jishan were the criminals responsible for Ruan Lingyu's death, one being greedy and shameless, and the other having found a new love. Therefore, she traveled all the way from Hunan to Nanjing to ask her cousin, Mr. Li, to introduce her to the film industry so that she could avenge Ruan Lingyu.

Regarding the actions of this young woman from Hunan, Liu Feifei, many people in society will surely say that she is obsessed with movies. What does Ruan Lingyu's death have to do with her? Yet, she resolutely decided to sacrifice herself to avenge Ruan Lingyu. This kind of behavior is indeed too peculiar. What else could it be but movie fanaticism? However, Liu Feifei's actions, while certainly a bit peculiar, do seem like she has indeed become a movie fan. But upon closer inspection, Liu Feifei's behavior may contain other meanings as well.

Liu Feifei's sympathy for Ruan Lingyu and her admiration for Ruan Lingyu's art are certainly important factors. But beyond this factor, we suspect that she also holds a desire to seek justice for oppressed women. She firmly believes that Ruan Lingyu's suicide was caused by the oppression of Zhang Damin and Tang Jishan. Therefore, in order to seek justice for oppressed women, she decided to sacrifice herself to avenge Ruan Lingyu. If our speculation is correct, then we cannot simply dismiss Liu Feifei's behavior as movie fanaticism. It is actually very meaningful and worthy of praise.

However, here we want to tell Liu Feifei that it was Zhang Damin and Tang Jishan who oppressed Ruan Lingyu. But in today's Chinese society, Ruan Lingyu is not the only woman being oppressed, and Zhang Damin and Tang Jishan are not the only men oppressing women. Therefore, we believe that if Liu Feifei truly holds the desire to seek justice for oppressed women, avenging Zhang Damin and Tang Jishan is not enough. We should be bolder and resist all men in society who oppress women. Only in this way can women achieve true liberation.

One Night at Yueyang Tower 225

— Zhen

The vast river water reveals undulating waves. A light boat floats in the middle of the stream, gently teasing the waves like a water gull.

"We're arriving soon, passengers please get up and pack your luggage!" the sailor shouted.

Startled awake, I blankly lowered my head for a moment, pushed open the boat window and looked out. The towering "Jintan" (brand name) billboard in the sky stared with a smiling face as it overlooked the passing river and the bright setting sun.

Walking out of the cabin door, I released the stuffy air that had been pent up in my chest all day, feeling as if I had lost several pounds.

Guanyin Island, shrouded in the evening mist, seemed to be swallowed up by the rushing water, while Chenglingji, facing it across the bank, flashed an arrogant face, guarding this gateway that must be passed through.

Page 18

This is the confluence of the Yangtze River and the Xiang River. To reach Yueyang, one must go upstream. Therefore, when our boat turned into the adverse current, two sailors took up their poles, and two sailors went ashore to pull the tow rope. In the late autumn lakeside of Dongting, the reed flowers were bleak and the mud was knee-deep. The sailors pulling the tow rope struggled forward on this difficult journey.

The boat berthed at the lower bay of Yueyang City. The lake was already deeply locked in a sheet of evening mist. Junshan Island, rising from the center of the lake, only existed in our vague memories.

There was a burst of noise on the boat as everyone collected their money, each carrying their large and small packages and rushing ashore.

On the shore, the pebbles, rounded and clear from the impact of the lake waves, had a magical power that made us stumble at every step. The remaining light of a few fishing lamps peeking out from the thatched sheds further confused our desired destination.

Finally, we found the gate of Yueyang Tower. The gate was gloomy like a bottomless cave. Even though it was a clear day, the stone steps were covered with mud. There was no light, only a flickering kerosene lamp, as small as a firefly, lined up at the end of the city gate.

"Friend, be careful not to fall." Someone walking ahead warned me like this.

Turning onto an uneven street, the sparse streetlights and desolate shadows presented an image of economic depression. It was only seven or eight o'clock, but some of the shops were already closed tightly. Only a few tea houses and hotels still had some noise to decorate the night of this ancient city.

Mr. So-and-so and I stayed in a small inn in Chaijia Ridge. The broken windows and walls were pathetically small, and cobwebs were stretched everywhere. The traces of travelers' graffiti on the walls were all blurred. A musty smell was rampant throughout the room.

"This room hasn't been inhabited for a long time, has it?"

We sat down, drank a cup of tea, and asked this question.

"Business has been bad recently. No one has any business, no matter which one!" the tea attendant said, then sighed.

"Why don't you clean up? This way, no one will come!"

"How can we not clean up? 'A house needs people to make it.' It's been a long time since we've had a guest. The boss has dismissed several of us employees. Now there's only me left. I have to cook, how can I have time!" He said tiredly.

"If there are more guests, who will serve them?"

"When there are many, the boss and the landlady will come to help."

Finally, we changed to a room, and the price increased to one thousand four hundred, but it was cleaner than the original one. After eating a simple dinner, because we had to catch the train the next day, Mr. So-and-so suggested taking a night tour of Yueyang Tower.

Guided by the tea attendant, we stepped onto the stone steps, turned a bend, and arrived at the main hall of Lu Zu. The Buddhist statues and shrines were brand new. The plaques and couplets had very few ancient relics. From this, we knew that they had all been destroyed in the fires of war. However, the "believers" came in droves to burn incense and pray, and the monks were busy ringing bells and drumming, as if the prosperity and market of Yueyang had moved here! It can be seen how superstitious the foolish men and women are in this decadent Chinese society, relying on the gods to save them from the depths of misery! Turning to the open space on the third floor, under a weeping electric light, the dark lake water floated together with the sky. The words carved on the surrounding walls were mottled and had turned white. Even Fan Zhongyan's preface carved on the wooden planks seemed to have a sense of vicissitudes.

It was already ten o'clock when we returned to the inn. The next day, before dawn, we left this ancient city that stole its reputation.

Students Returning Home 226

— Liu Ying

The Sorrow of a Great Talent 227

— Ye Fei

The great talent has been an apprentice in this barbershop for almost two years, but the whip marks on his body are increasing with the years, months, days, and hours. By now, he himself does not know how many whip marks he has on his body. And no one else has ever counted them for him, and even if there were such a person who would count them for him, they would not necessarily be able to count them clearly. Because every day, when he is lazy or makes a mistake (in his master's eyes), he has to be beaten by his master. But every day after he is beaten, he is never seen to cry even once. This is not because he can't cry, but because his master doesn't allow him to cry. If he cries! There is a risk of being beaten even more severely! He understands that an apprentice can only endure. Even if he is wronged by the master, he can only swallow his anger and has no right to spit it out. Therefore, the master is only allowed to beat himself, but he is not allowed to cry out. However, the great talent is not afraid to cry; he knows that it is useless to shed these extra tears in front of the master. His master will not necessarily soften because of this; on the contrary, it is simply equivalent to begging for a living.

He remembers that since the year his mother put on a new blue cloth gown, the first new clothes he had ever worn in his life, and lit a pair of five-lamp candles in front of the family altar, he kowtowed three times to the family altar, then bowed to the people in the surrounding villages, and followed a cousin to leave home. It seemed that at this time, his mother, who was not very old but looked very old on her face, still saw him off for a while. As the boat left the dock, his mother, with tears in her eyes, urged him like this: "Great talent, go with your uncle. There is no food for you to eat at home. Go to Shanghai and eat your fill! But be careful in everything, and listen to your master. Remember what your mother says. Shanghai is a good place. See how hard it is in the countryside! I hope that when you have finished your apprenticeship and come back, you will bring some glory to your dead father. Then my half-life of suffering will not have been in vain..." She cried before she could finish speaking.

At this time, the great talent seemed to have no feeling. He did not laugh, nor did he cry, nor did he speak. His eyes were only staring blankly at his mother's thin face, which was covered with tears. He did not understand his mother's heart. She wanted him to go to learn a trade, so why was she crying now? He had not analyzed any of his mother's words in his own heart. He only knew that Shanghai was a good place, and he should be happy to have the opportunity to go to this good place. Although he had thought that he would be separated from his mother, with whom he depended for life, and that this separation would be so far away for three years; at that time, he was indeed somewhat sad, but this only sorrow was ultimately buried by this dream of longing.

In that year, he entered this barbershop, and at the same time lit red candles that were dozens of times larger than the pair of five-lamp candles lit in front of his own family altar, and then respectfully kowtowed three times to a big man. After his cousin taught him to call him master, he entrusted his entire fate to that master. So, every day, he swept the floor, washed towels, wiped the equipment, boiled water, and arranged the towels, starting his apprenticeship. In the blink of an eye, two years passed, and only sadness and pain continued to increase on his body, and the so-called dream of longing was completely shattered! He felt that his mother's words were wrong, what about eating his fill, good place, and bringing some glory to his dead father!

Returning to Mother's Home 228

— Pin Yun

Aunt Siwei hobbled out of Uncle Siwei's two black-lacquered doors, with only a faded red cloth package, the one she had when she got married, hanging on her wrist. Her face was very unpleasant as she staggered towards the path outside the village in the twilight.

In the evening, wisps of curling smoke floated from the rooftops of the village houses, poetically drifting straight into the sky, slowly dissipating along with the light clouds across the blue sky. At this time, the air in the village was particularly quiet. Even the little dogs sleeping at the door were too lazy to raise their heads. Only the villagers, covered in muddy stains, returned from their work in the fields, and on their way home, they often turned their heads to scan Aunt Siwei, who was walking unsteadily with her head down like a homeless dog, with strange eyes.

Arriving at her mother's house, a sudden burst of sorrow assaulted Aunt Siwei's heart, and her eyes seemed to be covered by a gloomy cloud of sorrow. She remembered the decline and dilapidation of her mother's house, and her father's early death. A string of bitter tears could not help but flow from her eyes. However, what could she do? If she didn't go to her mother's house, where else could she go? So, she stretched out her trembling hand and gently pushed open the moldy, old, and dilapidated bamboo door.

"Grandma, the aunt has come back... Aunt, why are you back so late? Alone?... "The sister-in-law was feeding the chickens in the courtyard and hurriedly put down the chicken feed and came forward to greet her. "What's wrong? Aunt, are your eyes bad? Why are they swollen and painful like two rotten walnuts?"

Aunt Siwei did not reply at all. She strode into the courtyard with all her might, threw the faded red cloth package on the dirty mud floor, and fell into her mother's arms, crying out like a child who had been wronged.

The sister-in-law was also stunned and did not even bother to close the bamboo door. She followed closely behind her aunt, crossed the courtyard, and startled the chickens that were pecking at food in the yard.

"Qiao'er, why are you crying so much!... Did you suffer any grievances on the way, or in your husband's house?..."

After a bout of weeping, Aunt Siwei seemed to feel a little tired. The crying was slightly softer than before, and her throat was gasping as if she could not breathe. She tilted her head and looked at her mother's senile appearance: the sparse hair on her temples was white like a few strands of silver silk, and the hand that was stroking her hair was also dry and thin like firewood. So, her heart felt sad and painful again, and tears welled up in her eyes like mountain springs.

"Qiao'er, what exactly happened? Tell your mother... "The old woman's voice trembled a little, and she became more anxious.

"Mom, I... That damned man... doesn't want me anymore. He's going to marry... a young vixen, saying that I just eat his family's food and can't... give... him a son!... "Aunt Siwei said intermittently, and at the same time, the gasping in her throat became even more rapid.

"That's outrageous! The Siwei family must have gone crazy! Actually, the aunt is only in her thirties. Who dares to say that she won't be able to have children in the future!" the sister-in-law exclaimed angrily. "Their ancestors didn't accumulate virtue and had no luck to have children. Who can they blame! Aunt, don't cry. Tomorrow, we'll gather some people to go to the Siwei family and argue with him. Does he think he can abuse people just because he has some stinking money? If not, there are still village rules in the village..."

The mother's head swayed like a willow in the wind, and she could not say half a word. It was clear that her elderly heart was as broken as Aunt Siwei's.

Aunt Siwei lived in her mother's house like this, for one month, two months, three months... At first, the sister-in-law was still very sympathetic to her and took care of her. However, as time went on, although her mother still loved her in the same way, the sister-in-law's attitude towards her became as thin as the morning mist. Sometimes, she even used many small incidents to insinuate her with the tone of scolding livestock, mocking her, as if she were not a member of the family! When the neighbors secretly discussed her, and when the sister-in-law ridiculed her, her chest felt as painful as if it had been pierced by a poisonous arrow. She felt that she was the most miserable person in the world! She could only secretly shed hot tears to vent her full of bitterness.

Yao Xiao'an, Wang Pingqiu, Qilin Leopard

Zhong Xi (1040) 11:00 PM to 12:00 AM

Opening "Song of Grieving for Spring"

Fair face gaunt, thinking of embracing spring. Husband and wife separated, failing to live up to spring. Thinking back to when the wedding night was filled with passionate love, the hibiscus curtains warm, spending the night in spring. Under the dressing table, slowly watching, eyebrows painted lightly, a smile containing spring. A moment of gold wasted away, now as cold as ice and ashes, doubly grieving for spring. Cunning brother, partial to eloquent words, containing sour plums, bitterly meeting spring. The aunt doesn't understand, who can redeem it? Can I be heartless, not cherishing spring? New people have new smiles, how can the old wife weep away the remnant of spring? The lovely daughter is lively and diligently asks, "Daddy, why are you separated and abandoning spring?" Tears, bitterness, like a dream, hating that there are no comforting words, falsely scolding spring. The curtains are down, the sound is silent, the incense burns out, too lazy to stir the spring in the silent furnace. Tasting medicine, wondering who will take care of me, too much illness, after all, little return to spring. Vainly living through the years, no other thoughts, flesh and blood children are like the spring in my eyes. The calamity of Huang Yang can be expected, reunion like the spring in the mirror. Heaven and earth are not eternal, this lingering hatred misunderstands youth. It is truly like fallen grass wilting in spring.

Shen Bao Local Supplement Movie Special

On the Establishment of the Ruan Lingyu Acting Award 233

— Ling He

A few days ago, this magazine had an article "Preliminary Proposal for Establishing the Ruan Lingyu Acting Award." At that time, after reading it, I had a feeling of excitement and anxiety. In order to promote the efforts of Chinese film actors in acting and the health of their lifestyle, to eliminate the pessimistic atmosphere, and also to commemorate the death of a generation of artist Ruan Lingyu, the establishment of this award does have its great significance. Therefore, at that time I was quite excited. But I also considered this proposal myself: It is very difficult for the Chinese film industry to have an organization, which everyone knows very clearly. For example, there used to be a Film Association, but because it was subject to some objective resistance, everyone was not enthusiastic, and it soon disappeared. Later, there was a film tea party, which was just a casual chat, but if everyone was enthusiastic and caring, it was not without benefits, and it was possible to talk about things that were beneficial to everyone. But I don't know how, it soon disappeared invisibly. Now there is nothing. Film practitioners are all groping independently in the dark. They don't communicate with each other. Even an organization like a film library or a film research association is not possible to realize. In view of these facts, I can't help but worry about the establishment of this acting award, although this is due to excessive excitement.

Sure enough, after that article was proposed, there was no significant response. In particular, the gentlemen of the film industry did not put forward concrete opinions, although the author of that article was expecting a lively discussion. Of course, Chinese people have always believed in the philosophy of life of "sweeping the snow in front of their own doors," but for this matter that is for others and for themselves, it is not appropriate to be too silent, right? But I always believe that the success of a social undertaking must have a few foolish people who are doing their best to do it. At least I personally have to provide some opinions as a reference.

Regarding the realization of this award, the most important thing is the source of funding. Of course, if one person is awarded each year, and if the award is 200 yuan, then there must be a fund of 2,000 yuan. (If 2,000 yuan is deposited for a long time, it can get 200 yuan at an annual interest rate of 1%). This is not a small number, and no one will be willing to donate it alone. Moreover, individual donations are not as meaningful as social fundraising. Therefore, I believe that the method of raising funds should be based on the principle of truly obtaining it from the social audience. Because only enthusiastic audiences are strong supporters of Chinese films, and only a broad audience is the most sincere protector of film actors, and also a strong monitor of their lives and behaviors. Then, under this principle, I think there are three ways that can work.

First, fundraising. Establish a fundraising committee and collect donations separately in various theaters, schools and other educational organizations.

Second, with the consent of Lianhua Company, donate the screening of Ruan Lingyu's most outstanding works, with the ticket revenue as part of the fund.

Third, perform a play. Since Ruan Lingyu's death, general amusement parks have regarded her as the same way to produce wealth as Ge Ruixiong or Huang Hui, and everyone has adapted her death into dramas such as "The Fall of a Fragrant Jade." Needless to say, in those timely scripts, it is very unlikely that we can ask for a true analysis of Ruan Lingyu's outlook on life and the cause of her death. On the contrary, it is just a mess like traveling to the underworld. Then, if we can perform a play well to commemorate Ruan Lingyu, it is definitely not without meaning, and at the same time, this income will be used to raise funds.

As mentioned above, they are all within the possible range. What is left is the trouble of implementation. Perhaps in addition to this, there are better ways. This is waiting for enthusiastic discussion by people who care about Chinese films.

Editor's Note: Since the publication of Mr. Xudong's "Preliminary Proposal for Establishing the Ruan Lingyu Acting Award" in this magazine on March 19, this magazine has received several letters, all expressing their agreement and willing to do their best to donate, but hoping that this magazine will lead the planning and implementation, so that a meaningful plan will not end up in vain, which is very gratifying. However, it is a pity that no concrete opinions have been put forward, and the respondents are few, which shows that people in society do not yet have a deep understanding of the event. Recalling the day of Ms. Ruan's burial, men and women in Shanghai went to watch the funeral, and the road was filled with people. From this, we know that there are many idle people watching the excitement, but there are still few people who take out their empty bodies and do some useful things for the social crowd, which is very disappointing. Fortunately, Mr. Ling showed us this article, and we are eager to expose it in the hope that someone will be inspired to rise up. We especially hope that film practitioners, for the sake of their own interests, can put forward considerable concrete measures or contribute useful opinions (the text does not have to be published, but it is enough to provide it for reference). Not smart.

Film Reviews

Review of "Slick Spirit Medium" 234

— Ji Han

Their Big Moment

——Da Shanghai Screening

If we admit that this film was made because of the two embarrassing faces of ZaSu Pitts and Zasu Pitts and Slim Summerville, then people's first attention is on their acting skills. Generally speaking, ZaSu Pitts is not incapable of acting. The development of her personality can indeed become a typical representative of ordinary honest women. Therefore, when she plays a supporting role in certain works, she often makes people laugh, and at the same time makes people deeply appreciate the goodness and loveliness of human nature. But profit-seeking film merchants often injure actors in order to reluctantly cater to the audience's preferences. For example, ZaSu Pitts has to repeatedly produce some nonsensical and humorous short films, which is an example. So under the control of these vulgar filmmakers, she lost the audience's sympathy, and she was just a vulgar thing in Hollywood. As for Slim Summerville, who has acted in humorous films such as "Legal Eagles," he has never had better results. Perhaps some people say that he doesn't make a lot of noise, but he can't go deep into the real life. All he can do is a face that seems to be an honest person and seems to be a fool, using a relatively static posture to make people laugh. However, now is the time when people regard humor as humor, so some people are quite satisfied with him. Because of this, his works are also welcomed by a part of the audience.

Now let's look at this "talking nonsense" "Slick Spirit Medium" Here is another unrealistic and almost mythical story, which cannot arouse our much interest. The content is also empty, vulgar and boring. What good plays can be seen at the session, not to mention that the director is just a plain and unremarkable narration of the story. Although it can sometimes make people laugh, the whole play cannot arouse people's emotional resonance. ZaSu Pitts and Slim Summerville are just repeating the old tunes and repeating their original acting skills, without any new tricks. They were not originally talented actors, not to mention that they are here under a director with not much creative ability? The result is conceivable. Although this is a work made because of the actors, their acting skills cannot make people laugh heartily.

Movie Chat 235

— Luo Ping

Since Carl Laemmle first put the names of stars on the screen, the star system has been quickly established; it has been popular until now.

However, no one can deny that the star system has its own drawbacks. To give an example, because too much emphasis is placed on the "star system," the death of a certain actress has at least given film merchants who rely on this system a not small loss.

Recently, directors Shen Xicen and Shi Dongwang solved the problem of ranking by the number of strokes in their surnames or the order of their appearances. Although this is not a fundamental solution, this new and progressive method is worth recommending to every film director.

American producer Samuel Goldwyn is offering a reward of £20,000 for a simple story for his brother Conrad's new film.

There is now a prevailing criticism of tragic films, saying that sad themes will make many petty citizens increase their decadent and depressed emotions, and even believe that they "poison" the audience in the same way as pornographic films. However, who can deny that as a film art that reflects the reality of "life", it is impossible to have "happy" themes in this tragic real world?

The Director of "Escape" 237

The director of "Escape" is Mr. Yue Feng, who is very young, short in stature, and has a Chaplin-style mustache on his lips. Therefore, generally speaking, "Escape" is the first and most powerful and successful exposé film in the history of Chinese films! At least; the unique style of this film can awaken the audience's ears and eyes.

The Hate of the Fallen Country of India (Clive of India) (10) 238

— Mao De

And if Miye Fa, out of fear or insincerity, fails to defect as scheduled, then the entire plan will fail. Clive, in distress and worry, his wife came in. She was holding a bunch of flowers in her hand. She said in a low voice: "After you left, I was just thinking of going to church." Clive nodded and said: "Suddenly it has been two years." That's right, it's been two years. On this day two years ago, they buried the little Clive in a church cemetery in London. Clive thought of it and couldn't help but sadly said: "Margretti, I don't know if you will hate me. I have caused you such a great loss and suffered such great pain. I only know how to take, but you are giving."

Margretti also sadly said: "Robert, please don't do this. You are also giving. We will safely get through all the difficulties, won't we?" Clive took her hand and kissed it. She asked again: "How long will this war take?" Clive said: "One month... two months... it's not certain. Sala Ut Du La and his army are stationed opposite Parasi. Miye Fa is also there. He promised to defect and help me." Margretti said: "Do you believe what he says?" Clive said: "At least I believe what he says?" Clive said: "At least I believe his greed, he wants to be emperor. Maybe this time we will win without a fight! Then peace, hometown, wealth, and settlement are all ours"

Margretti leaned on her husband. Clive asked sadly again: "Margretti, tell me one thing. Suppose I am standing at a fork in the road. If I advance and win, there is naturally nothing to say. If I lose, that is our destruction. Sala Ut Du La has no mercy for men, women, and children... Tell me, do you allow me or not, let me advance automatically?" Margretti looked at his face, hesitated for a while, and then said: "Robert, you know, I am very simple, but I know that no one can stop a man like you."

Clive nodded gratefully. She is always understanding. She has never violated his wishes. The horn sounded again outside, and he had to go out. He hugged her tightly in his arms, tenderly for a while, and then said in a low voice: "Goodbye." The two of them had to separate, as if some force was tearing them apart. Clive then hurried away.

Clive and his team waited quietly for ten days, hiding in the forest, not daring to cross the river. Those days were days of fear and panic. If Mill Yefa betrayed his promise, then the tragic consequences he would get would far outweigh the Black Hole of Calcutta incident recorded in history. At that time, Sala Ut Du La put 146 British people in a cave, which had only one small hole for air. So after a day, the people inside suffocated to death, leaving only three or four people struggling for their lives. Because of this inhuman behavior, Clive decided to ally with Mill Yefa to remove this demon Sala Ut Du La. If he could not remove him, the British would never have a peaceful day in India. But this was an extremely risky move.

At this time, the Governor specially ran from Fort Saint David to check the situation. He brought a pair of Margretti's letters. Clive took the letter, put it in his pocket, and did not open it to read. The Governor asked him how the future was. Clive answered casually, Mill Yefa. But he can go to the front at any time.

Shen Bao Architecture Weekly

Recent Trends in Residential Architecture 239

— Xi Hao

The rapid advancement of architecture in recent years has truly surpassed other applied sciences. Especially in residential architecture, there has been significant progress not only in technology and form but also new developments in the most important fundamental concepts and design. This is truly a characteristic of 20th-century architecture and an unprecedented bright page in architectural history.

In the 19th century and before, engineers' understanding of the meaning of "residence" was indeed very superficial. They believed that a "residence" was merely a place for people to return to at night after labor. Therefore, the "residential" buildings of that time were only used to shield from wind and rain and prevent unexpected attacks. Although the exteriors had magnificent stone heights, engineers have now recognized a deeper meaning in 20th-century "residences." Modern "residences" are not only for resting weary humans but also permanent comforters of mankind. This is indeed the main distinguishing point between residential architecture of the past and present.

Harmony and delicacy are the characteristics of new-style residences. The first success of harmony lies in the appropriate proportions of each part of the residence. In past residential buildings, deep consideration was often not given to the volume of each room, resulting in inconvenience when put to use. For example, living rooms were excessively large, and factories were too small. This kind of disproportion not only caused excessive consumption of materials but also depreciated the value of the entire building. The advantage of new-style residences is the commensurate proportion of each part's volume, ensuring that the homeowner can easily manage everything and obtain a comfortable aesthetic.

The color design of the interior and exterior of residences was never considered by engineers in the 19th century, which was indeed a great mistake. Color has a great impact on people's feelings. The appropriate arrangement of colors, especially indoors where sunlight is reflected, can bring pleasure and comfort to the entire mind. Now, the architectural community in various countries has engineers specializing in the study of color design in architecture. This is indeed unprecedented. Due to the rapid adoption of light metals, the successful arrangement of beautiful artificial pigments for construction, aluminum foil, zinc paint, etc., are now very commonly used.

Modern engineers have abandoned the generally old-fashioned and clumsy thick walls in the design of residences. Because of the continuous invention of new building materials, the formerly bulky pillars have been replaced by light steel frame combination beams. In general, in new-style residences, you will sometimes find it strange that there is not a single pillar. It turns out that these pillars are sometimes cleverly hidden inside the walls, and sometimes they are omitted as much as possible and replaced with delicate beams. In this way, the expansion of the location is quite large, and at the same time, the beauty of the entire residence is greatly increased.

Now, almost every kind of building material is tested by a material testing machine. Their properties and the strength they can withstand are all recorded in detail. Therefore, when planning a residence, it can be carried out very accurately, without the need for excessively large safety factors. In this way, the cost of construction will be more economical, and the waste of materials can be reduced to a minimum.

Multi-story residential buildings are now on the rise, but although the number of floors has increased, the height of each floor has been reduced compared to past buildings. Engineers have generally recognized that this type of low-rise building is easier to design and is also very strong. Tall floors are really not necessary, because after studying the light and volume ratios, the advantages of low-rise buildings have been proven, and there is also considerable evidence for the comfort they provide to people's spirits.

In addition to the above, new-style residences are also becoming more and more perfect in terms of internal equipment. The convenience of water and electricity pipe connections, and the thoroughness of disinfection designs, are now available in larger residences, with entertainment facilities, home movie theaters, or small-scale sports fields, allowing people to obtain the necessary comfort.

In short, modern engineers have a deeper understanding of the meaning of "residence." Modern "residences" not only solve the problem of "living" but are also gradually becoming permanent comforters of people's minds.

Material Science for Construction (7) 240

— Zhu Zhenmu

Section 6: Electric Furnace Method

The electric furnace method is the best steelmaking method. The steel obtained by the above methods can also be remelted by this method to achieve cleanliness.

The steps of smelting are divided into three steps: oxidation, reduction, and completion.

(1) Oxidation - During oxidation, pig iron ore and lime are placed in the furnace together. After heat radiation and high heat, the iron ore releases oxygen and undergoes oxidation, causing impurities such as silicon, magnesium, sulfur, and phosphorus to become oxides, which combine to form a black slag.

(2) Reduction - A mixture of five parts of lime and one part of feldspar powder semi-liquid is combined with one-fourth part of white coal to form a reducing agent, which is put into the furnace. Close off external air from entering, so that the temperature inside the furnace gradually decreases. When the steel is reduced, the slag will appear yellowish-brown, and at the same time, a calcium carbide odor will be released, which is sufficient to indicate.

(3) Completion - To complete the steel, it is necessary to add various useful materials, such as nickel, manganese, chromium, carbon, and tungsten.

In total, the time taken for the three steps is about four or five hours for each ton of steel smelted, and the electricity consumption is about 100 to 200 kilowatt-hours.

Therefore, although this method can obtain better steel quality and does not require other fuels, the electricity consumption is extremely high, and there is much heat waste and high electricity costs, so it is not very economical. The Shanghai Central Research Institute Steelmaking Plant has this equipment, and the Shanghai Steelmaking Plant also has a small-scale one. (End of Chapter 4)

Chapter 5: On Steel

Section 1: The advantages and disadvantages of impurities contained in steel are sufficient to affect its hardness, force, toughness, and other properties. The following describes several common substances.

(1) Carbon - When the carbon content in iron is 1.25%, it can enhance the force of iron. However, if it is not evenly distributed and forms granules, it will only make the iron hard but not tough, so attention must be paid.

The carbon content in steel is generally inconsistent. It is about 0.05% to 1.5% in mild steel, 0.15% to 0.25% in structural steel, 0.35% to 0.8% to 1.2% in medium steel, and 0.6% to 1.5% in steel for tools such as knives and saws. Knives must be strong, so more carbon is needed. For example, the steel used for safety razors has a special name called high-grade carbon steel, without which a sharp blade cannot be obtained. Structural steel only needs to be durable and strong, so not much carbon is needed.

(2) Silicon - The silicon content in ordinary steel is about 0.20%, while special steel is no more than 1.0% to 4.0%; the silicon content in structural steel is about 1.9%, and the silicon content in spring and automobile steel is also about 2.0%.

(3) Phosphorus - Steel with a high phosphorus content is brittle and does not last long, so the degree is 0.5% to 1.0%. If it exceeds this, it will be unusable. (To be continued)

Overview of the Planned Construction of an Office Building by the Beijing-Shanghai-Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways Bureau 241

— Dong Dayou

Introduction

The Railways Bureau, in view of the high cost of rent for the current office space and the inconvenience of the location, which affects the coordination of work between various departments and makes it difficult to achieve ideal work efficiency, has proposed a plan to build its own office building to bring together all departments of the bureau in one place, so as to achieve the effect of arms and fingers. Currently, the Traffic and Police Departments are attached to the North Station, the Shanghai Hospital of the Two Railways and other departments are located in the Riverside Building on North Suzhou Road. This arrangement is only a temporary expedient. In the future, when the plan is realized, they will all be moved into the building. The following is an overview of the designed building project.

(1) Location

The new building will be located opposite the North Station, facing the southwest corner of Jielu and Baoshan Road, with an estimated area of 300 feet wide and 100 feet deep. There will be a gap behind the building, enough to park 50 cars. Since the new building is close to the North Station, the convenience of traffic will undoubtedly benefit public affairs handling and contact.

The construction of this building is only a part of the future station's grand plan. The station in the grand plan will be located at the intersection of Baoshan Road and Jielu. The required area will be expanded several times. The current plan includes offices, hotels, freight rooms, and all railway business equipment. This plan is based on the opinion of the Engineering Department of the Two Railways Bureau, and the construction of this office building is the beginning of the entire plan.

(2) Architectural Overview

The building is ten stories high, with twelve stories in the middle. It is 260 feet long and 60 feet deep. The exterior walls are made of artificial stone, the lower part is made of sesame stone, and the wall surface is decorated with simple Chinese-style carvings, which are solid and simple, meeting the requirements of modern architecture without losing the flavor of Chinese architecture.

The building is divided into a central part and two wings. The central part is wider and has three elevators. There are also escalators, toilets, information workers, and night offices, all facing north. The important offices are concentrated in the south-facing central part, but regardless of whether they face south or north, each quarter of the rooms are open to the air on all sides, so there is no darkness, and the air is very sufficient.

The entire building is made of reinforced concrete, the inner walls are made of hollow bricks, the corridors are paved with polished stone, and the office floors are paved with rubber blocks. Each floor also has a fire shelter for the placement of important documents and materials. Sanitary and electrical equipment is available in each department.

The entrance gate is located in the middle of the building, facing Jielu to the south. The hospital occupies the west, with a separate west entrance, isolated from other departments. The cafeteria, which can accommodate 300 people, is located on the tenth floor. Other facilities such as the library and telephone room are all available. The distribution of each floor is recorded below.

Ground Floor Traffic Department Hospital

Second Floor Traffic Department Hospital

Third Floor Police Department Hospital

Fourth Floor General Affairs Department

Fifth Floor General Affairs Department Director's Office

Sixth Floor Accounting Department

Seventh Floor Accounting Department Engineering Department

Eighth Floor Mechanical Engineering Department

Ninth Floor Materials Department Materials Testing Institute

Tenth Floor Cafeteria

Eleventh Floor Blueprint Room Drawing Room

Twelfth Floor Machine Room Wireless Room Telephone Room
